## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[EntityGraphReduceTask] --> B{reduce_legs?}
    B -->|True| C[requires: ETLEntityTask]
    B -->|False| C
    C --> D[Run Spark Job on EMR]
    D --> E[app_options: env, output path, reduce_legs]
    E --> F{reduce_legs?}
    F -->|True| G[Output: entity_graph_reduce_task.parquet]
    F -->|False| H[Output: entity_graph_reduce_task_with_legs.parquet]
```

## Diagram 3

stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Initialize
